</a>\n         </sup>\n         <br/>\n         1790\xe2\x80\x931960\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-55">\n          <a href="#cite_note-55">\n           [52]\n          </a>\n 1990\xe2\x80\x932000\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-57">\n          <a href="#cite_note-57">\n           [54]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n         <br/>\n         <a </table>\n      <p>\n       As of the\n       <a href="/wiki/2010_United_States_Census" title="2010 United States Census">\n        2010 United States Census\n       </a>\n       , there were 204,214 people residing in the city. 50.6% were\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/African_American" title="African American">\n        Black or African American\n       </a>\n       , 40.8%\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/White_American" title="White American">\n        White\n       </a>\n       , 5.0%\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Asian_American" title="Asian American">\n        Asian\n       </a>\n       , 0.3%\n       <a href="/wiki/Native_Americans_in_the_United_States" title="Native Americans in the United States">\n        Native American\n       </a>\n       , 0.1%\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Pacific_Islands_American" title="Pacific Islands American">\n        Pacific Islander\n       </a>\n       , 3.6% of some other race and 2.3%\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Multiracial_American" title="Multiracial American">\n        of two or more races\n       </a>\n       . 6.3% were\n       <a href="/wiki/Hispanic_and_Latino_Americans" title="Hispanic and Latino Americans">\n        Hispanic or Latino\n       </a>\n       (of any race).\n      </p>\n      <div class="thumb tleft">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Race_and_ethnicity_2010-_Richmond_(5560433168).png">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3009" data-file-width="3009" height="220" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a2/Race_and_ethnicity_2010-_Richmond_%285560433168%29.png/220px-Race_and_ethnicity_2010-_Richmond_%285560433168%29.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a2/Race_and_ethnicity_2010-_Richmond_%285560433168%29.png/330px-Race_and_ethnicity_2010-_Richmond_%285560433168%29.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a2/Race_and_ethnicity_2010-_Richmond_%285560433168%29.png/440px-Race_and_ethnicity_2010-_Richmond_%285560433168%29.png 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Race_and_ethnicity_2010-_Richmond_(5560433168).png" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Map of racial distribution in Richmond, 2010 U.S. Census. Each dot is 25 people:\n         <span style="color:#ff0000">\n          <b>\n           White\n          </b>\n         </span>\n         ,\n         <span style="color:#0000ff">\n          <b>\n           Black\n          </b>\n         </span>\n         ,\n         <span style="color:#00ff80">\n          <b>\n           Asian\n          </b>\n         </span>\n         ,\n         <span style="color:#ff8000">\n          <b>\n           Hispanic\n          </b>\n         </span>\n         or\n         <b>\n          Other\n         </b>\n         (yellow)\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       As of the census\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-GR8_58-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-GR8-58">\n         [55]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       of 2000, there were 197,790 people, 84,549 households, and 43,627 families residing in the city. The population density was 3,292.6 people per square mile (1,271.3/km\xc2\xb2). There were 92,282 housing units at an average density of 1,536.2 per square mile (593.1/km\xc2\xb2). The racial makeup of the city was 38.3%\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/White_(U.S._Census)" title="White (U.S. Census)">\n        White\n       </a>\n       , 57.2%\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/African_American_(U.S._Census)" title="African American (U.S. Census)">\n        African American\n       </a>\n       , 0.2%\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Native_American_(U.S._Census)" title="Native American (U.S. Census)">\n        Native American\n       </a>\n       , 1.3%\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Asian_(U.S._Census)" title="Asian (U.S. Census)">\n        Asian\n       </a>\n       , 0.1%\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Pacific_Islander_(U.S._Census)" title="Pacific Islander (U.S. Census)">\n        Pacific Islander\n       </a>\n       , 1.5% from\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Race_(United_States_Census)" title="Race (United States Census)">\n        other races\n       </a>\n       , and 1.5% from two or more races.\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hispanic_(U.S._Census)" title="Hispanic (U.S. Census)">\n        Hispanic\n       </a>\n       or\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Latino_(U.S._Census)" title="Latino (U.S. Census)">\n        Latino\n       </a>\n       of any race were 2.6% of the population.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       There were 84,549 households out of which 23.1% had children under the age of 18 living with them, 27.1% were married couples living together, 20.4% had a female householder with no husband present, and 48.4% were non-families. 37.6% of all households were made up of individuals and 10.9% had someone living alone who was 65 years of age or older. The average household size was 2.21 and the average family size was 2.95.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       In the city, the age distribution of the population shows 21.8% under the age of 18, 13.1% from 18 to 24, 31.7% from 25 to 44, 20.1% from 45 to 64, and 13.2% who were 65 years of age or older. The median age was 34 years. For every 100 females there were 87.1 males. For every 100 females age 18 and over, there were 83.5 males.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The median income for a household in the city was $31,121, and the median income for a family was $38,348. Males had a median income of $30,874 versus $25,880 for females. The per capita income for the city was $20,337. About 17.1% of families and 21.4% of the population were below the poverty line, including 32.9% of those under age 18 and 15.8% of those age 65 or over.\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Crime">\n        Crime\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Richmond,_Virginia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Crime">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       During the late 1980s and early 1990s, Richmond experienced a spike in overall crime, in particular, the city\'s\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Murder_rate" title="Murder rate">\n        murder rate\n       </a>\n       . The city had 93 murders for the year of 1985, with a murder rate of 41.9 killings committed per 100,000 residents. Over the next decade, the city saw a major increase in total\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Homicides" title="Homicides">\n        homicides\n       </a>\n       . In 1990 there were 114 murders, for a murder rate of 56.1 killings per 100,000 residents. There were 120 murders in 1995, resulting in a murder rate of 59.1 killings per 100,000 residents, one of the highest in the United States.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Disaster_Center_59-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Disaster_Center-59">\n         [56]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       In 2004,\n       <a href="/wiki/Morgan_Quitno_Press" title="Morgan Quitno Press">\n        Morgan Quitno Press\n       </a>\n       ranked Richmond as the ninth (out of 354) most dangerous city in the\n       <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">\n        United States\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Morgan_Quitno_60-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Morgan_Quitno-60">\n         [57]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In 2005, Richmond was ranked as the fifth most dangerous city overall and the 12th most dangerous\n       <a href="/wiki/Metropolitan_area" title="Metropolitan area">\n        metropolitan area\n       </a>\n       in the United States.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-cqpress_61-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-cqpress-61">\n         [58]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-62">\n        <a href="#cite_note-62">\n         [59]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-63">\n        <a href="#cite_note-63">\n         [60]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The following year, Richmond saw a decline in crime, ranking as the 15th most dangerous city in the United States. By 2008, Richmond\'s position on the list had fallen to 49th.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-2008_rankings_64-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-2008_rankings-64">\n         [61]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       By 2012, Richmond was no longer in the \'top\' 200.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-2012_rankings_65-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-2012_rankings-65">\n         [62]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Richmond\'s rate of major crime, including violent and property crimes, decreased 47 percent between 2004 and 2009 to its lowest level in more than a quarter of a century.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Williams_Bowes_66-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Williams_Bowes-66">\n         [63]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Various forms of crime tend to be declining, yet remaining above state and national averages.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CLR_67-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-CLR-67">\n         [64]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In 2008, the city had recorded the lowest homicide rate since 1971.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Williams_Reed_68-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Williams_Reed-68">\n         [65]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       <a href="/wiki/Federal_Bureau_of_Investigation" title="Federal Bureau of Investigation">\n        FBI\n       </a>\n       <a href="/wiki/Uniform_Crime_Reports" title="Uniform Crime Reports">\n        Uniform Crime Reports\n       </a>\n       for Richmond for the year of 2013:\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-FBI_UCR_69-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-FBI_UCR-69">\n         [66]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <table class="wikitable">\n       <tr>\n        <th>\n        </th>\n        <th>\n         City of Richmond only\n        </th>\n        <th>\n        <td>\n         1,128\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         90.8\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         Aggravated assault\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         623\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         1,575\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         126.8\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         Property crime\n        </td>\n   <td>\n         Motor vehicle theft\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         938\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         1,899\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         152.9\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       In recent years, as in many other American cities, Richmond has witnessed a rise in homicides.\n       <i>\n        The Richmond Times-Dispatch\n       </i>\n       reported 61 murders in Richmond in 2016, marking it "the city\'s deadliest year in a decade."\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-70">\n        <a href="#cite_note-70">\n         [67]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Religion">\n        Religion\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Richmond,_Virginia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Religion">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:St._John%27s_Church_in_Richmond,_VA_(2011)_IMG_4046.JPG">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3240" data-file-width="4320" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/St._John%27s_Church_in_Richmond%2C_VA_%282011%29_IMG_4046.JPG/220px-St._John%27s_Church_in_Richmond%2C_VA_%282011%29_IMG_4046.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/St._John%27s_Church_in_Richmond%2C_VA_%282011%29_IMG_4046.JPG/330px-St._John%27s_Church_in_Richmond%2C_VA_%282011%29_IMG_4046.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/St._John%27s_Church_in_Richmond%2C_VA_%282011%29_IMG_4046.JPG/440px-St._John%27s_Church_in_Richmond%2C_VA_%282011%29_IMG_4046.JPG 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:St._John%27s_Church_in_Richmond,_VA_(2011)_IMG_4046.JPG" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         <a href="/wiki/St._John%27s_Episcopal_Church_(Richmond,_Virginia)" title="St. John\'s Episcopal Church (Richmond, Virginia)">\n          St. John\'s Episcopal Church\n         </a>\n         , built in 1741, is the oldest church in the city\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       In 1786, the\n       <a href="/wiki/Virginia_Statute_for_Religious_Freedom" title="Virginia Statute for Religious Freedom">\n        Virginia Statute for Religious Freedom\n       </a>\n       , penned in 1779 by\n       <a href="/wiki/Thomas_Jefferson" title="Thomas Jefferson">\n        Thomas Jefferson\n       </a>\n       , was adopted by the Virginia General Assembly in Richmond. The site is now commemorated by the\n       <a href="/wiki/First_Freedom_Center" title="First Freedom Center">\n        First Freedom Center\n       </a>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Richmond has several historic churches. Because of its early English colonial history from the early 17th century to 1776, Richmond has a number of prominent Anglican/Episcopal churches including\n       <a href="/wiki/Monumental_Church" title="Monumental Church">\n        Monumental Church\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/St._Paul%27s_Episcopal_Church_of_Richmond,_Virginia" title="St. Paul\'s Episcopal Church of Richmond, Virginia">\n        St. Paul\'s Episcopal Church\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Saint_John%27s_Church,_Richmond,_Virginia" title="Saint John\'s Church, Richmond, Virginia">\n        St. John\'s Episcopal Church\n       </a>\n       . Methodists and Baptists made up another section of early churches, and\n       <a href="/wiki/First_Baptist_Church_(Richmond,_Virginia)" title="First Baptist Church (Richmond, Virginia)">\n        First Baptist Church of Richmond\n       </a>\n       was the first of these, established in 1780. In the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Reformed_church" title="Reformed church">\n        Reformed church\n       </a>\n       tradition, the first Presbyterian Church in the City of Richmond was First Presbyterian Church, organized on June 18, 1812. On February 5, 1845,\n       <a href="/wiki/Second_Presbyterian_Church_(Richmond,_Virginia)" title="Second Presbyterian Church (Richmond, Virginia)">\n        Second Presbyterian Church of Richmond\n       </a>\n       was founded, which was a historic church where\n       <a href="/wiki/Stonewall_Jackson" title="Stonewall Jackson">\n        Stonewall Jackson\n       </a>\n       attended and was the first\n       <a href="/wiki/Gothic_architecture" title="Gothic architecture">\n        Gothic\n       </a>\n       building and the first\n       <a href="/wiki/Gas_lighting" title="Gas lighting">\n        gas-lit\n       </a>\n       church to be built in Richmond.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-71">\n        <a href="#cite_note-71">\n         [68]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a href="/wiki/St._Peter%27s_Church_(Richmond,_Virginia)" title="St. Peter\'s Church (Richmond, Virginia)">\n        St. Peter\'s Church\n       </a>\n       was dedicated and became the first Catholic church in Richmond on May 25, 1834.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-72">\n        <a href="#cite_note-72">\n         [69]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The city is also home to the historic\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Cathedral_of_the_Sacred_Heart_in_Richmond" title="Cathedral of the Sacred Heart in Richmond">\n        Cathedral of the Sacred Heart\n       </a>\n       which is the\n       <a href="/wiki/Mother_church" title="Mother church">\n        mother church\n       </a>\n       for the\n       <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Diocese_of_Richmond" title="Roman Catholic Diocese of Richmond">\n        Roman Catholic Diocese of Richmond\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-73">\n        <a href="#cite_note-73">\n         [70]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div class="thumb tleft">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Cathedral_of_the_sacred_heart.JPG">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1024" data-file-width="768" height="293" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6f/Cathedral_of_the_sacred_heart.JPG/220px-Cathedral_of_the_sacred_heart.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6f/Cathedral_of_the_sacred_heart.JPG/330px-Cathedral_of_the_sacred_heart.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6f/Cathedral_of_the_sacred_heart.JPG/440px-Cathedral_of_the_sacred_heart.JPG 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Cathedral_of_the_sacred_heart.JPG" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         The\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Cathedral_of_the_Sacred_Heart_in_Richmond" title="Cathedral of the Sacred Heart in Richmond">\n          Cathedral of the Sacred Heart\n         </a>\n         , dedicated in 1906\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       The\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Oldest_synagogues_in_the_United_States" title="Oldest synagogues in the United States">\n        first Jewish congregation\n       </a>\n       in Richmond was Kahal Kadosh Beth Shalom. Kahal Kadosh Beth Shalom was the sixth congregation in the United States. By 1822\xc2\xa0K.K. Beth Shalom members worshipped in the first synagogue building in Virginia. They eventually merged with\n       <a href="/wiki/Congregation_Beth_Ahabah" title="Congregation Beth Ahabah">\n        Congregation Beth Ahabah\n       </a>\n       , an offshoot of Beth Shalom. There are two Orthodox Synagogues, Keneseth Beth Israel and Chabad of Virginia.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-74">\n        <a href="#cite_note-74">\n         [71]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       There is an Orthodox\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Yeshivah" title="Yeshivah">\n        Yeshivah\n       </a>\n       K\xe2\x80\x9312 school system known as Rudlin Torah academy, which also includes a post high-school program. There are two Conservative synagogues, Beth El and Or Atid. There are three Reform synagogues, Bonay Kodesh,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-75">\n        <a href="#cite_note-75">\n         [72]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Beth Ahabah and Or Ami. Along with such religious congregations, there are a variety of other Jewish charitable, educational and social service institutions, each serving the Jewish and general communities. These include the Weinstein Jewish Community Center, Jewish Family Services, Jewish Community Federation of Richmond and\n       <a href="/wiki/Richmond_Jewish_Foundation" title="Richmond Jewish Foundation">\n        Richmond Jewish Foundation\n       </a>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Due to the influx of German\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Immigrants" title="Immigrants">\n        immigrants\n       </a>\n       in the 1840s,\n       <a href="/wiki/St._John%27s_United_Church_of_Christ,_Richmond,_Virginia" title="St. John\'s United Church of Christ, Richmond, Virginia">\n        St. John\'s German Evangelical church\n       </a>\n       was formed in 1843. Saints Constantine and Helen Greek Orthodox Cathedral held its first worship service in a rented room at 309 North 7th Street in 1917. The cathedral relocated to 30 Malvern Avenue in 1960 and is noted as one of two Eastern Orthodox churches in Richmond and home to the annual Richmond Greek Festival.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-76">\n        <a href="#cite_note-76">\n         [73]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       There are seven current\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Masjid" title="Masjid">\n        masjids\n       </a>\n       in the Greater Richmond area, with three more currently in construction,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-77">\n        <a href="#cite_note-77">\n         [74]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-78">\n        <a href="#cite_note-78">\n         [75]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-79">\n        <a href="#cite_note-79">\n         [76]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       accommodating the growing Muslim population, the first one being Masjid Bilal.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-80">\n        <a href="#cite_note-80">\n         [77]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-81">\n        <a href="#cite_note-81">\n         [78]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In the 1950s, Muslims from the East End got organized under Nation of Islam (NOI). They used to meet in Temple #24 located on North Avenue. After the NOI split in 1975, the Muslims who joined mainstream Islam, start meeting at Shabaaz Restaurant on Nine Mile Road. By 1976, the Muslims used to meet in a rented church. They tried to buy this church, but due to financial difficulties the Muslims instead bought an old grocery store at Chimbarazoo Boulevard, the present location of Masjid Bilal. Initially, the place was called "Masjid Muhammad #24". Only by 1990 did the Muslims renamed it to "Masjid Bilal". Masjid Bilal was followed by the Islamic Center of Virginia, ICVA\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-82">\n        <a href="#cite_note-82">\n         [79]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       masjid. The ICVA was established in 1973 as a non profit tax exempt organization. With aggressive fundraising, ICVA was able to buy land on Buford road. Construction of the new masjid began in the early 1980s. The rest of the five current masjids in the Richmond area are Islamic Center of Richmond (ICR)\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-83">\n        <a href="#cite_note-83">\n         [80]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       in the west end, Masjid Umm Barakah\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-84">\n        <a href="#cite_note-84">\n         [81]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       on 2nd street downtown, Islamic Society of Greater Richmond (ISGR)\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-85">\n        <a href="#cite_note-85">\n         [82]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       in the west end, Masjidullah\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-86">\n        <a href="#cite_note-86">\n         [83]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       in the north side, and Masjid Ar-Rahman\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-87">\n        <a href="#cite_note-87">\n         [84]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       in the east end.\n      </p>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:WattsHallUnionPresbyterianSeminary.JPG">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2448" data-file-width="3264" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/be/WattsHallUnionPresbyterianSeminary.JPG/220px-WattsHallUnionPresbyterianSeminary.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/be/WattsHallUnionPresbyterianSeminary.JPG/330px-WattsHallUnionPresbyterianSeminary.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/be/WattsHallUnionPresbyterianSeminary.JPG/440px-WattsHallUnionPresbyterianSeminary.JPG 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:WattsHallUnionPresbyterianSeminary.JPG" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Watts Hall at\n         <a href="/wiki/Union_Presbyterian_Seminary" title="Union Presbyterian Seminary">\n          Union Presbyterian Seminary\n         </a>\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       <a href="/wiki/Hinduism" title="Hinduism">\n        Hinduism\n       </a>\n       is actively practiced, particularly in suburban areas of Henrico and Chesterfield. Some 6,000 families of Indian descent resided in the Richmond Region as of 2011. Hindus are served by several temples and cultural centers. The two most familiar are the Cultural Center of India (CCI) located off of Iron Bridge Road in Chesterfield County and the Hindu Center of Virginia in Henrico County which has garnered national fame and awards for being the first\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/LEED_certified" title="LEED certified">\n        LEED certified\n       </a>\n       religious facility in the commonwealth.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       <a href="/wiki/Seminary" title="Seminary">\n        Seminaries\n       </a>\n       in Richmond include: the school of theology at\n       <a href="/wiki/Virginia_Union_University" title="Virginia Union University">\n        Virginia Union University\n       </a>\n       ; a Presbyterian seminary,\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Union_Theological_Seminary_%26_Presbyterian_School_of_Christian_Education" title="Union Theological Seminary &amp; Presbyterian School of Christian Education">\n        Union Presbyterian Seminary\n       </a>\n       , and the\n       <a href="/wiki/Baptist_Theological_Seminary_at_Richmond" title="Baptist Theological Seminary at Richmond">\n        Baptist Theological Seminary at Richmond\n       </a>\n       . The\n       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=McCollough_Theological_Seminary&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="McCollough Theological Seminary (page does not exist)">\n        McCollough Theological Seminary\n       </a>\n       of the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_House_of_Prayer_For_All_People" title="United House of Prayer For All People">\n        United House of Prayer For All People\n       </a>\n       is located in the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Church_Hill,_Richmond,_Virginia" title="Church Hill, Richmond, Virginia">\n        Church Hill\n       </a>\n       neighborhood of the city.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Bishops that sit in Richmond include those of the Episcopal Diocese of Virginia (the denomination\'s largest); the Richmond Area of the United Methodist Church (Virginia Annual Conference), the nation\'s second-largest and one of the oldest. The Presbytery of the James\xe2\x80\x94Presbyterian Church (USA) \xe2\x80\x93 also is based in the Richmond area.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Diocese_of_Richmond" title="Roman Catholic Diocese of Richmond">\n        Roman Catholic Diocese of Richmond\n       </a>\n       was canonically erected by\n       <a href="/wiki/Pope_Pius_VII" title="Pope Pius VII">\n        Pope Pius VII\n       </a>\n       on July 11, 1820. Today there are 235,816 Catholics at 146 parishes in the Diocese of Richmond.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-88">\n        <a href="#cite_note-88">\n         [85]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The city of Richmond is home to 19 Catholic parishes.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-89">\n        <a href="#cite_note-89">\n         [86]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Cathedral_of_the_Sacred_Heart_in_Richmond" title="Cathedral of the Sacred Heart in Richmond">\n        Cathedral of the Sacred Heart\n       </a>\n       is home to the current bishop\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Francis_Xavier_DiLorenzo" title="Francis Xavier DiLorenzo">\n        Most Reverend Francis Xavier DiLorenzo\n       </a>\n       who was appointed by\n       <a href="/wiki/Pope_John_Paul_II" title="Pope John Paul II">\n        Pope John Paul II\n       </a>\n       on March 31, 2004.\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Economy">\n        Economy\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Richmond,_Virginia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Economy">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Tobacco_Warehouse_Interior,_Richmond,_Virginia.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="502" data-file-width="800" height="138" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c5/Tobacco_Warehouse_Interior%2C_Richmond%2C_Virginia.jpg/220px-Tobacco_Warehouse_Interior%2C_Richmond%2C_Virginia.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c5/Tobacco_Warehouse_Interior%2C_Richmond%2C_Virginia.jpg/330px-Tobacco_Warehouse_Interior%2C_Richmond%2C_Virginia.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c5/Tobacco_Warehouse_Interior%2C_Richmond%2C_Virginia.jpg/440px-Tobacco_Warehouse_Interior%2C_Richmond%2C_Virginia.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Tobacco_Warehouse_Interior,_Richmond,_Virginia.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Richmond tobacco warehouse ca. 1910s\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Richmond\'s strategic location on the\n       <a href="/wiki/James_River" title="James River">\n        James River\n       </a>\n       , built on undulating hills at the rocky\n       <a href="/wiki/Atlantic_Seaboard_fall_line" title="Atlantic Seaboard fall line">\n        fall line\n       </a>\n       separating the\n       <a href="/wiki/Piedmont_region_of_Virginia" title="Piedmont region of Virginia">\n        Piedmont\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Tidewater_region" title="Tidewater region">\n        Tidewater regions\n       </a>\n       of Virginia, provided a natural nexus for the development of commerce. Throughout these three centuries and three modes of transportation, the downtown has always been a hub, with the Great Turning Basin for boats, the world\'s only triple crossing of rail lines, and the intersection of two major interstates.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Law and finance have long been driving forces in the economy.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-90">\n        <a href="#cite_note-90">\n         [87]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The city is home to both the\n       <a href="/wiki/United_States_Court_of_Appeals_for_the_Fourth_Circuit" title="United States Court of Appeals for the Fourth Circuit">\n        United States Court of Appeals for the Fourth Circuit\n       </a>\n       , one of 13\n       <a href="/wiki/United_States_courts_of_appeals" title="United States courts of appeals">\n        United States courts of appeals\n       </a>\n       , and the\n       <a href="/wiki/Federal_Reserve_Bank_of_Richmond" title="Federal Reserve Bank of Richmond">\n        Federal Reserve Bank of Richmond\n       </a>\n       , one of 12\n       <a href="/wiki/Federal_Reserve_System" title="Federal Reserve System">\n        Federal Reserve Banks\n       </a>\n       , as well as offices for international companies such as\n       <a href="/wiki/Genworth_Financial" title="Genworth Financial">\n        Genworth Financial\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/CapitalOne" title="CapitalOne">\n        CapitalOne\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Philip_Morris_USA" title="Philip Morris USA">\n        Philip Morris USA\n       </a>\n       , and numerous other banks and brokerages. Richmond is also home to four of the largest law firms in the United States:\n       <a href="/wiki/Hunton_%26_Williams" title="Hunton &amp; Williams">\n        Hunton &amp; Williams\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/McGuireWoods" title="McGuireWoods">\n        McGuireWoods\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Williams_Mullen" title="Williams Mullen">\n        Williams Mullen\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=LeClairRyan&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="LeClairRyan (page does not exist)">\n        LeClairRyan\n       </a>\n       . Another law firm with a major Richmond presence is\n       <a href="/wiki/Troutman_Sanders" title="Troutman Sanders">\n        Troutman Sanders\n       </a>\n       , which merged with Richmond-based Mays &amp; Valentine LLP in 2001.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Since the 1960s Richmond has been a prominent hub for advertising agencies and advertising related businesses. As a result of local advertising agency support,\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/VCU" title="VCU">\n        VCU\n       </a>\n       \'s graduate advertising school (VCU Brandcenter) is consistently ranked the No. 1 advertising graduate program in the country.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-91">\n        <a href="#cite_note-91">\n         [88]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Richmond is home to the rapidly developing Virginia BioTechnology Research Park,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-92">\n        <a href="#cite_note-92">\n         [89]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       which opened in 1995 as an incubator facility for biotechnology and pharmaceutical companies. Located adjacent to the Medical College of Virginia (MCV) Campus of\n       <a href="/wiki/Virginia_Commonwealth_University" title="Virginia Commonwealth University">\n        Virginia Commonwealth University\n       </a>\n       , the park currently\n       <sup class="noprint Inline-Template" style="white-space:nowrap;">\n        [\n        <i>\n         <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Manual_of_Style/Dates_and_numbers#Chronological_items" title="Wikipedia:Manual of Style/Dates and numbers">\n          <span title="The time period mentioned near this tag is ambiguous. (January 2010)">\n           when?\n          </span>\n         </a>\n        </i>\n        ]\n       </sup>\n       has more than 575,000 square feet (53,400\xc2\xa0m\n       <sup>\n        2\n       </sup>\n       ) of research, laboratory and office space for a diverse tenant mix of companies, research institutes, government laboratories and non-profit organizations. The\n       <a href="/wiki/United_Network_for_Organ_Sharing" title="United Network for Organ Sharing">\n        United Network for Organ Sharing\n       </a>\n       , which maintains the nation\'s\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Organ_transplant" title="Organ transplant">\n        organ transplant\n       </a>\n       waiting list, occupies one building in the park.\n       <a href="/wiki/Philip_Morris_USA" title="Philip Morris USA">\n        Philip Morris USA\n       </a>\n       opened a $350 million research and development facility in the park in 2007. Once fully developed, park officials expect the site to employ roughly 3,000 scientists, technicians and engineers.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Richmond\'s revitalized downtown includes the Canal Walk, a new Greater Richmond Convention Center, and expansion on both\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/VCU" title="VCU">\n        VCU\n       </a>\n       campuses. A new performing arts center,\n       <a href="/wiki/Richmond_CenterStage" title="Richmond CenterStage">\n        Richmond CenterStage\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-93">\n        <a href="#cite_note-93">\n         [90]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       opened on September 12, 2009.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-centerstage_94-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-centerstage-94">\n         [91]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The complex included a renovation of the Carpenter Center and construction of a new multipurpose hall, community playhouse, and arts education center in parts of the old Thalhimers department store.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-95">\n        <a href="#cite_note-95">\n         [92]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Richmond is also fast-becoming known for its food scene, with several restaurants in the Fan, Church Hill, Jackson Ward and elsewhere around the city generating regional and national attention for their fare.\n       <i>\n        <a href="/wiki/Departures_(magazine)" title="Departures (magazine)">\n         Departures\n        </a>\n       </i>\n       magazine named Richmond "The Next Great American Food City" in August 2014.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-96">\n        <a href="#cite_note-96">\n         [93]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Departures_food_97-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Departures_food-97">\n         [94]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       while Metzger Bar &amp; Butchery made its "Best New Restaurants: 12 To Watch" list.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-98">\n        <a href="#cite_note-98">\n         [95]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a href="/wiki/Microbrewery" title="Microbrewery">\n        Craft beer\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Liquor" title="Liquor">\n        liquor\n       </a>\n       production is also growing in the River City, with twelve micro-breweries in city proper; the oldest is Legend Brewery, founded in 1994. Three\n       <a href="/wiki/Distillation" title="Distillation">\n        distilleries\n       </a>\n       , Reservoir Distillery, Belle Isle Craft Spirits and James River Distillery, were established in 2010, 2013 and 2014, respectively.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Additionally, Richmond is gaining attention from the film and television industry, with several high-profile films shot in the metro region in the past few years, including the major motion picture\n       <i>\n        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Lincoln_(2012_film)" title="Lincoln (2012 film)">\n         Lincoln\n        </a>\n       </i>\n       which led to\n       <a href="/wiki/Daniel_Day-Lewis" title="Daniel Day-Lewis">\n        Daniel Day-Lewis\n       </a>\n       \'s third Oscar,\n       <i>\n        <a href="/wiki/Killing_Kennedy_(film)" title="Killing Kennedy (film)">\n         Killing Kennedy\n        </a>\n       </i>\n       with\n       <a href="/wiki/Rob_Lowe" title="Rob Lowe">\n        Rob Lowe\n       </a>\n       , airing on the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/National_Geographic_Channel" title="National Geographic Channel">\n        National Geographic Channel\n       </a>\n       and\n       <i>\n        <a href="/wiki/Turn:_Washington%27s_Spies" title="Turn: Washington\'s Spies">\n         Turn\n        </a>\n       </i>\n       , starring\n       <a href="/wiki/Jamie_Bell" title="Jamie Bell">\n        Jamie Bell\n       </a>\n       and airing on\n       <a href="/wiki/AMC_(TV_channel)" title="AMC (TV channel)">\n        AMC\n       </a>\n       . In 2015 Richmond will be the main filming location for the upcoming\n       <a href="/wiki/PBS" title="PBS">\n        PBS\n       </a>\n       drama series\n       <i>\n        Mercy Street\n       </i>\n       , which will premiere in Winter 2016. Several organizations, including the Virginia Film Office and the Virginia Production Alliance, along with events like the Richmond International Film Festival and French Film Festival, continue to put draw supporters of film and media to the region.\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Fortune_500_companies_and_other_large_corporations">\n        Fortune 500 companies and other large corporations\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Richmond,_Virginia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Fortune 500 companies and other large corporations">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:City_of_Richmond_Business_District.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2148" data-file-width="3072" height="154" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2d/City_of_Richmond_Business_District.jpg/220px-City_of_Richmond_Business_District.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2d/City_of_Richmond_Business_District.jpg/330px-City_of_Richmond_Business_District.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2d/City_of_Richmond_Business_District.jpg/440px-City_of_Richmond_Business_District.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:City_of_Richmond_Business_District.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Six\n         <a href="/wiki/Fortune_500" title="Fortune 500">\n          Fortune 500\n         </a>\n         companies are headquartered in the Richmond area\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       The Greater Richmond area was named the third-best city for business by\n       <a href="/wiki/MarketWatch" title="MarketWatch">\n        MarketWatch\n       </a>\n       in September 2007, ranking behind only the Minneapolis and Denver areas and just above Boston. The area is home to six\n       <a href="/wiki/Fortune_500" title="Fortune 500">\n        Fortune 500\n       </a>\n       companies: electric utility\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Dominion_Resources" title="Dominion Resources">\n        Dominion Resources\n       </a>\n       ;\n       <a href="/wiki/CarMax" title="CarMax">\n        CarMax\n       </a>\n       ;\n       <a href="/wiki/Owens_%26_Minor" title="Owens &amp; Minor">\n        Owens &amp; Minor\n       </a>\n       ;\n       <a href="/wiki/Genworth_Financial" title="Genworth Financial">\n        Genworth Financial\n       </a>\n       ;\n       <a href="/wiki/MeadWestvaco" title="MeadWestvaco">\n        WestRock\n       </a>\n       Company;\n       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=McKesson_Medical-Surgical&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="McKesson Medical-Surgical (page does not exist)">\n        McKesson Medical-Surgical\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Markel_Corporation" title="Markel Corporation">\n        Markel Corporation\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Altria_Group" title="Altria Group">\n        Altria Group\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Fortune500_6-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Fortune500-6">\n         [6]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       However, only Dominion Resources and WestRock Company are headquartered within the city of Richmond; the others are located in the neighboring counties of\n       <a href="/wiki/Henrico_County,_Virginia" title="Henrico County, Virginia">\n        Henrico\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Hanover_County,_Virginia" title="Hanover County, Virginia">\n        Hanover\n       </a>\n       . In 2008, Altria moved its corporate HQ from New York City to Henrico County, adding another Fortune 500 corporation to Richmond\'s list. In February 2006,\n       <a href="/wiki/MeadWestvaco" title="MeadWestvaco">\n        MeadWestvaco\n       </a>\n       announced that they would move from\n       <a href="/wiki/Stamford,_Connecticut" title="Stamford, Connecticut">\n        Stamford, Connecticut\n       </a>\n       , to Richmond in 2008 with the help of the Greater Richmond Partnership,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ATL_Business_Chronicle_-_MWV_99-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-ATL_Business_Chronicle_-_MWV-99">\n         [96]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       a regional economic development organization that also helped locate\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Aditya_Birla_Minacs" title="Aditya Birla Minacs">\n        Aditya Birla Minacs\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Yahoo_Finance_-_Minacs_100-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Yahoo_Finance_-_Minacs-100">\n         [97]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Amazon.com" title="Amazon.com">\n        Amazon.com\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Retailing_Today_-_Amazon_101-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Retailing_Today_-_Amazon-101">\n         [98]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Honeywell_International" title="Honeywell International">\n        Honeywell International\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Business_Facilities_-_Honeywell_102-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Business_Facilities_-_Honeywell-102">\n         [99]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       to the region. In July 2015, MeadWestvaco merged with Georgia-based Rock-Tenn Company creating\n       <a href="/wiki/WestRock" title="WestRock">\n        WestRock\n       </a>\n       Company.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Other\n       <a href="/wiki/Fortune_500" title="Fortune 500">\n        Fortune 500\n       </a>\n       companies, while not headquartered in the area, do have a major presence. These include\n       <a href="/wiki/SunTrust_Banks" title="SunTrust Banks">\n        SunTrust Bank\n       </a>\n       (based in\n       <a href="/wiki/Atlanta" title="Atlanta">\n        Atlanta\n       </a>\n       ),\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Capital_One_Financial_Corporation" title="Capital One Financial Corporation">\n        Capital One Financial Corporation\n       </a>\n       (officially based in\n       <a href="/wiki/McLean,_Virginia" title="McLean, Virginia">\n        McLean, Virginia\n       </a>\n       , but founded in Richmond with its operations center and most employees in the Richmond area), and the medical and pharmaceutical giant\n       <a href="/wiki/McKesson_Corporation" title="McKesson Corporation">\n        McKesson\n       </a>\n       (based in San Francisco). Capital One and Altria company\'s Philip Morris USA are two of the largest private Richmond-area employers.\n       <a href="/wiki/DuPont" title="DuPont">\n        DuPont\n       </a>\n       maintains a production facility in South Richmond known as the Spruance Plant.\n       <a href="/wiki/UPS_Freight" title="UPS Freight">\n        UPS Freight\n       </a>\n       , the less-than-truckload division of\n       <a href="/wiki/United_Parcel_Service" title="United Parcel Service">\n        UPS\n       </a>\n       and formerly known as\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Overnite_Transportation" title="Overnite Transportation">\n        Overnite Transportation\n       </a>\n       , has its corporate headquarters in Richmond.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Other companies based in Richmond include chemical company\n       <a href="/wiki/NewMarket_Corporation" title="NewMarket Corporation">\n        NewMarket\n       </a>\n       ;\n       <a href="/wiki/Brink%27s" title="Brink\'s">\n        Brink\'s\n       </a>\n       , a security and armored car company;\n       <a href="/wiki/Estes_Express_Lines" title="Estes Express Lines">\n        Estes Express Lines\n       </a>\n       , a freight carrier,\n       <a href="/wiki/Universal_Corporation" title="Universal Corporation">\n        Universal Corporation\n       </a>\n       , a tobacco merchant;\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Cavalier_Telephone_and_TV" title="Cavalier Telephone and TV">\n        Cavalier Telephone\n       </a>\n       , now Windstream, a telephone, internet, and digital television provider formed in Richmond in 1998;\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Cherry_Bekaert_%26_Holland" title="Cherry Bekaert &amp; Holland">\n        Cherry Bekaert &amp; Holland\n       </a>\n       , a top 30 accounting firm serving the\n       <a href="/wiki/Southeastern_United_States" title="Southeastern United States">\n        Southeast\n       </a>\n       ; the law firm of\n       <a href="/wiki/McGuireWoods" title="McGuireWoods">\n        McGuireWoods\n       </a>\n       ; and\n       <a href="/wiki/Media_General" title="Media General">\n        Media General\n       </a>\n       , a company specializing in broadcast media.\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Arts_and_culture">\n        Arts and culture\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Richmond,_Virginia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Arts and culture">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 210px; float: right; clear: right; margin:0 0 1.0em 1.0em">\n       <caption>\n        External video\n       </caption>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n         <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Downtown_Richmond_VA.jpg">\n          <img alt="Downtown Richmond VA.jpg" data-file-height="2448" data-file-width="3264" height="158" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8a/Downtown_Richmond_VA.jpg/210px-Downtown_Richmond_VA.jpg"
